CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Backorder %]
 AS [Measures].[Backorder]/[Measures].[Counting Cells], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Stock Status';     
 
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[PScore]
 AS Iif([Measures].[P Score Sales]=0,NULL,[Measures].[Weighted P Score Sales]/[Measures].[P Score Sales]), 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0.000;-#,##0.000", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Sales';    
     
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Consigned Onhand]
 AS [Measures].[Consigned Onhand - Fact Inv]/[Measures].[Period Distinct Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0;-#,##0", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Inventory';      
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[PScoreNew]
 AS Iif([Measures].[P Score Sales]=0,
NULL,([Measures].[PScore]-0.500)*[Measures].[Sales]/[Measures].[P Score Sales]), 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0.000;-#,##0.000", 
VISIBLE = 0 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Sales'; 
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Customer Count New]
 AS [Measures].[Customer Count] * [Customer].[Percent Credit], 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Count'  ;      
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[PScore Contribution]
 AS Iif([Measures].[P Score Sales]=NULL or [PScore]= NULL,
NULL,([Measures].[PScore]-0.500)*[Measures].[Sales]), 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0;-#,##0", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Sales';                                
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[On Hand Avg]
 AS [Measures].[On Hand]/[Measures].[Counting Cells], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Standard", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Stock Status';                                
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Availabe Avg]
 AS [Measures].[Available]/[Measures].[Counting Cells], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Standard", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Stock Status';        
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[NotAvailable%]
 AS [Measures].[Not Available]/[Measures].[Counting Cells], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Stock Status';            
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Revised %]
 AS [Measures].[Revised]/[Measures].[Receipt Lines], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact PO Receipts';                         
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Onhand]
 AS [Measures].[OnhandSum]/[Measures].[Period Distinct Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0;-#,##0", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Inventory';                
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Linked Value]
 AS [Measures].[Linked Value - Fact Inv]/[Measures].[Period Distinct Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Inventory';                
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Linked Onhand]
 AS [Measures].[Linked Onhand - Fact Inv]/[Measures].[Period Distinct Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0;-#,##0", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Inventory';                  
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Total Value]
 AS [Measures].[Total Value - Fact Inv]/[Measures].[Period Distinct Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Inventory';                    
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Annualized COGS]
 AS ([Measures].[Accounting Cost]/[Measures].[Complete Business Day])*[Measures].[Business Day T], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Inventory';                      
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Turns]
 AS (([Measures].[Accounting Cost]/[Measures].[Complete Business Day])*[Measures].[Business Day T])/([Measures].[Total Value - Fact Inv]/[Measures].[Period Distinct Count]), 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0.00;-#,##0.00", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Inventory';                            
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[GM %]
 AS [Measures].[Gross Margin]/[Measures].[Sales], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Sales';                            
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Accounting GM %]
 AS [Measures].[Accounting Gross Margin]/[Measures].[Sales], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Sales';                                   
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Stockout %]
 AS [Measures].[Stockout]/[Measures].[Counting Cells], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Stock Status';                                       
  

Scope(
       {
         [Measures].[Shipped Qty],
         [Measures].[Sales],
         [Measures].[Accounting Cost],
         [Measures].[Gross Margin]
       }
);                                       
  
End Scope;
